# **181 - To the Demonic Dragon Mountain Range 4**

「Sei, are you okay?」

「We picked this up for you.」

As I get carried by Brai away from the old demon tree, Rogyra and Jokon, who come along late, pick up my mithril shield for me.

Ah, thank goodness. I didn’t end up losing my precious equipment.

「Can you stand up?」

「Yeah, I just hurt my wrists.」

I put the shield into my storage and cast healing magic on my wrists.

I was hit by a greater impact than I expected, so the wrists of my hands, which were holding the shield, are sore. There doesn’t seem to be anything wrong with the bones, but I don’t think I’ll be able to fight any more battles today.

「Sei-kun, thank you so, so much. I’ll definitely thank you for this.」

「Yeah, you’re welcome. More importantly, let’s head to the night camp before it gets dark.」

「Yes, this way.」

Alright, I’ve managed to attract Elmefiora’s attention.

Result-wise, not only am I fine, I’ve also risked my life to get the medicinal herbs twice. Elmefiora must be feeling grateful and also indebted to me.

She said she would definitely thank me, so I think I can get my hopes up about this.

Under Elmefiora’s guidance, we head to the night camp.

「Here we are.」

The place to which Elmefiora led us appears to be an artificially managed area, as even though it’s in the middle of the forest, the trees have been cut down.

Looking closely, the ground is well-trodden and there are human footprints scattered here and there. I wonder if the parties coming to the demonic dragon mountain range have been camping here.

「We regularly sprinkle holy water around this area, so there’s little risk of monsters attacking us even at night. Just in case, we’ve also prepared some new holy water to sprinkle, so I think the risk of getting attacked by monsters is low.」

「…」

I know that Elmefiora is a member of a party skilled enough to come to the demonic dragon mountain range. But I wonder what the other members are doing? Many questions arise in my mind, but we can’t really question the client, so we silently prepare for the night camp.

I take out the holy water from my storage and have Frederie and the others sprinkle it on the surrounding area. I then take out some ingredients and prepare dinner. At night, we’ll just wrap ourselves with blankets and stay up so we can respond immediately in case we get attacked by monsters. As we busy ourselves with various things, the surrounding area gets dark in the blink of an eye.

The cries of animals echo eerily from the surrounding forest, so even though we have sprinkled holy water, we cannot say that we are absolutely safe here. Sigh, it has been a tough day, but I wonder if we will be able to sleep tonight.

「Brai, do you guys usually operate around this area?」

After dinner, there is nothing to do so I talk to Brai.

It seems that Elmefiora wants to hide her true identity, and Frederie gives off a somewhat hard to approach vibe, so the friendly Brai should be the best choice.

「Ah, we operated mainly in the Demonic Monkey Labyrinth in the south, but a lot of things happened, so we decided to leave the place for a while.」

「Oh, the Demonic Monkey Labyrinth. I heard that porters can make a lot of money there, so I’m thinking about trying going there too.」

「…I see, you can certainly make a lot of money there, but it’s also very dangerous.」

「I believe, I’ve heard that it’s a labyrinth with a high fatality rate.」

「That’s not it. No, the labyrinth itself is also dangerous, but the security there isn’t that great right now. Rowdy adventurers have formed factions and are fighting each other, and there’s no end to the skirmishes, you see.」

I see, even though the labyrinth is really dangerous in its own right, if there’s also the risk of getting attacked by fellow adventurers, that’d make that place even more dangerous. If Brai, who is a skilled adventurer, says so, maybe it’s best not to go there.

「Is it dangerous even for you guys? Can’t you dive into the labyrinth without getting involved with other adventurers?」

「You see, in the Demonic Monkey Labyrinth, demonic monkeys appear in troops of tens or even hundreds. You also need to form a party with dozens of people, so it’s not the kind of labyrinth that can be conquered by a small number of people.」

Are you serious? It seems like one hell of a labyrinth. Even if the monsters are only of single-digit ranks, if more than a hundred of them attack you at once, you probably won’t be able to deal with them. You’ll quickly run out of stamina and magical energy.

「But you’re a porter, so I think you’ll be highly regarded if you go there, Sei. They need porters to skin and bring back the demonic monkeys they defeat, after all.」

I see. To bring back a large number of demonic monkey skins, like hundreds of them, I guess they inevitably need a porter. Hmm, if I have time before the new year, I guess I’ll try stopping by there. If I carry myself as a porter rather than an adventurer, I wonder if the possibility of getting attacked will be lower.

Brai and the others seem to have made a considerable amount of money in the Demonic Monkey Labyrinth, so they don’t seem to be troubled with money. I guess Elmefiora was lucky. She was able to hire such kind, high-ranked adventurers. No, hold on a sec, we don’t know yet. Soon the surrounding area will be enveloped in darkness. Maybe they’re the kind of guys who would take advantage of this opportunity to attack Elmefiora in her sleep. We can’t let our guard down. Perhaps they’re just posing as kind adventurers now, but at night, they’ll turn into rape fiends. The surrounding area is a forest dominated by powerful monsters, so no one will come to our rescue. Damn it, I guess it’s going to be a long night.

「… Kuh.」

Suddenly, I feel a gaze on me, so I look around and meet Frederie’s eyes. His eyes are sharp, as if he was watching me.

Damn it, that guy, what manner of thing is he thinking about? If the four of them were to commit barbaric acts, there would be probably nothing Elmefiora and I could do about it. No, if she activates her powerful magic, I think even Frederie and the others won’t get out of it scot-free. She’s skilled enough to suppress the earth magic of that old demon tree, so if she gets serious, I think Elmefiora will be the most frightening person here. It’s hard to imagine them thoughtlessly laying their hand on her, but…

「Just to be on the safe side, we’ll take turns keeping watch.」

Following Frederie’s suggestion, we decide the order and take turns serving as night watchmen.

Regardless of the order, I don’t think I can afford to sleep. I need to keep an eye on not only monsters, but also their movements.

Come to think of it, Artemia once told me, didn’t she? That by using body manipulation skill, you can keep an eye on our surrounding area while sleeping. Alright, let’s take this opportunity to give it a try. If I can properly learn it, I should be able to make use of it in my future adventures, too.

Wrapped in a blanket, I pretend to be asleep and keep an eye on the surrounding area. Just to be on the safe side, I take out my red iron sword from my storage and slip it into my chest, getting ready to draw it at any moment.

As time passes and the night wears on, I gradually start to understand the tricks of manipulating the brain.

The area is completely silent, and perhaps thanks to the holy water, there is no sign of any monsters in the surrounding area.

Hmm, that Frederie, he’s staring intently at me.

While pretending to be asleep, I grip the hilt of my sword on my chest.

If you want to come, then come at me. I’ll take you on.

While erasing my presence, I get ready for battle.

The twilight lights up the sky, and the chirpings of birds start to echo in the distance.

Phew, it looks like I have worried too much. I’ve been on guard all through the night, but we make it through the night without anything happening.

Still, maybe because I’ve kept my brain on alert all night long, I feel like it hasn’t gotten much rest. As expected, it looks like it can’t get as much rest as when I have a good night’s sleep.

「Good morning, Elmefiora-san.」

「Yes, Sei-kun, good morning.」

Elmefiora also seems a little lethargic. Perhaps she, too, has been wary of us and was unable to sleep well.

「Fwah~, it’s morning already, huh.」

Perhaps because Brai and the others trust each other, they seem to have been able to sleep soundly.

Maybe these guys are really good people. No, we don’t know yet. We have to also consider the possibility that they will suddenly change once we have collected all the medicinal herbs. We can’t deny the possibility that their target is actually the medicinal herbs. At any rate, we can’t let my guard down completely.

After having a light breakfast, we decide to leave early in the morning for the place we’re headed for.

Once we get our hands on the last medicinal herb, the plan is to return to Tabrowa before the day is over. There is no time to relax.

「It’s over there.」

Under Elmefiora’s guidance, we come to a stop after walking for about two hours.

What she points to is a swamp-like place dotted with rugged rocks. Damn it, an unsettling vibe is hanging in the air. At any rate, this is the crucial moment. If we can somehow get through this, all that’s left is to go home.

「The propagating magic moss is growing on the rocks. Please don’t get too close to the swamp. As there are monsters that can use water magic from underwater.」

「So, what do you plan to do?」

「I want you to protect me while I collect the propagating magic moss.」

「…」

Hmm, I don’t know. Not only does it take a certain amount of physical ability to jump onto the rocks, there’s also the possibility that you’ll suddenly get attacked while you’re collecting the medicinal herbs, so I think it’s too dangerous for a magician like Elmefiora. Alright, let’s show off my usefulness one last time.

「Hold on a sec. I’ll collect the propagating magic moss.」

「Huh, Sei-kun?」

「Not only do I have experience in collecting it, I can also put the propagating magic moss into my storage and make a quick retreat. Frederie and the others will serve as my guards, and Elmefiora-san will stay here and support us with magic when the time calls for it.」

「Huh, b, but…」

「He’s right, that’s probably the most efficient way to do it.」

Elmefiora hesitates, but Brai agrees with me from the side, so it’s decided that we’ll adopt my plan.

Great, great, at one point I was worried about what would happen since I was the weakest person in this party, but with this, Elmefiora must have realized how reliable of a man I am. I deliberately step up to take on the dangerous role after all, she must be very grateful to me. But I mustn’t show it on my face. I have to maintain the attitude that I have no ulterior motives and just want to help Elmefiora who is in trouble.

「Elmefiora-san, no need to worry. I’ll definitely get the medicinal herbs.」

「Sei-kun…」

Alright, nailed it.

This Elmefiora, her eyes are getting a little watery, aren’t they? If it’s like this, I think I can get my hopes up for real. Perhaps I can expect a return that’s worth the risk.

「Alright, let’s go.」

I lead Frederie and the others into the swamp.

The presence of monsters… not good, it feels like they’re everywhere. But they shouldn’t be nearby. It feels like they’re watching us from somewhere far away.

At any rate, let’s not be greedy and pick only as much propagating magic moss as we need and retreat immediately.

「Everyone, please wait here.」

Right before the swamp, I decide to proceed by myself.

Rather than going to the rocky area with everyone, me going alone will be more agile and harder to be noticed by the enemy.

While using presence concealment, I jump onto the rocky area.

「This is…」

The rocky area is covered in a thick layer of propagating magic moss.

This is amazing, the quality must also be great.

I take out a barrel from my storage and start to put in the propagating magic moss I have scraped off with a knife, at that moment, a chill runs down my spine. What on earth is this…?

Clank, clank, clankkk.

「Huh…」

When I hear a metallic sound and turn around, I see a naked woman standing there, fighting Frederie and the others.

Huh…why is a person… N, no, the lower half of the woman’s body is a spider with yellow and black stripes. So this guy is a monster. Appraisal!

Scaly Skin Half-Human Jorogumo, Rank 79

Not good… It’s too strong, we have to retreat. But that guy is focused solely on Frederie and the others. I don’t know how much propagating magic moss she needs, but it’s too dangerous to come here again to get some more. While they’re fighting, I guess I’ll collect as much as I can.

One after another, I scrape off the propagating magic moss and put it into the barrel. Alright, this much should do. Time to retreat.

「Ugh.」

Suddenly, there is a magical energy reaction in the depths of the swamp, and bubbles begin to rise.

Things are getting too dangerous here. I use instant step and move away from the rocky area. I then regroup with Frederie and the others who are fighting the spider woman.

「I’ve got the medicinal herbs, time to retreat!」

I close in on the spider woman from behind, and while hitting her in the back with a surprise attack, I run towards where Elmefiora is.

「Sei!」

「Hmm… Geeh?!」

When I hear Brai’s voice and turn around, I see the spider woman has narrowed down her target on me  and is attacking me. target. Not good, looks like I’ve attracted too much of her hate.

The spider woman is naked above the waist, but has scales covering her skin. She looks to have high defensive power. Her hands have no fingers and are sharp like blades. She lifts the corners of her mouth in delight, and gleefully swings her blade down at me.

Clankkkkk.

「Kuh.」

I parry the spider woman’s right blade, which is swung down so fast… or rather, the attack is so powerful that I can’t block it. Then I dodge the left blade.

Swoosh.

Not good, I quickly lower my body and succeed in dodging it, but, although not completely, I can’t even stop her in her tracks.

Clank, clank.

Frederie and the others attack the spider woman from all sides. I’m holding the others back, so even if it’s just me alone, I have to get away from this place.

「Guah.」

「Tch.」

「Damn it.」

「This guy.」

I feel bad because it seems like I’m abandoning Frederie and the others who are engaging in a tough battle, but there’s nothing I can do here.

Using instant step, I get away from the front line and head towards where Elmefiora is.

Hmm, it looks like her magic is activating.

Boom, boom, boom, boooooooom!

「What on earth…?」

When I turn around, I see that walls of earth have risen up on all sides of the spider woman, trapping the monster inside. What incredible magic. The monster lets out cries as it attacks the walls.

「Now!」

Frederie and the others take advantage of this opportunity to successfully leave the front line. Having completed all of our missions, we head straight for Tabrowa.

# **182 - Completion of the Request**

Having successfully collected the medicinal herbs, we make our way through the forest at a fast pace towards Tabrowa.

Alright, we can see the town now. With this, we can be at ease… No, we don’t know yet. We must remain on guard against Frederick and the others until the very end. Even though it won’t get them much money, for them to accept a request to the dangerous demonic dragon mountain range, they must have some kind of ulterior motive.

「Phew, we’re finally back.」

「At one point, I wondered what would become of us.」

「The job wasn’t really worth it, but it was good enough to kill time.」

Huh, seriously?

As soon as we make it back to the town, Brai, Rogyra, and Jocon plop down with relieved looks on their faces. So they’re really just nice guys. There are also such adventurers in the world, huh.

First thing first, we head to the Adventurer’s Association to report the completion of the request. Frederie and the others receive their reward money, and with this, everything comes to an end.

「Brai, what are you guys going to do now?」

「Well, we don’t have any particular destination in mind, but for now, we’re planning to head to the territory capital in the west. We’ve had enough of the demonic dragon mountain range, after all.」

「I see, let’s meet again somewhere.」

I say goodbye to Brai and the others. After this, I’m going to visit a leech with Elmefiora and have them compound the medicinal herbs I have put into my storage. My reward will be the extra medicinal herbs, after all.

「Sei…」

「Oh, Frederie, I’ve truly been in your care. I misunderstood you…」

At the end, Frederie comes over to say goodbye to me.

As expected from a comrade of Brai and the others, Frederie is probably a good guy deep down. He’s just unsociable and has a mean look in his eyes. It seems there was no need to continue being on guard against him.

「… want to do it?」

「Like hell I do, you moron!!」

This guy, so the reason he has been staring intently at me all this time is because he’s been looking at me in a sexual light. In a way, it seems like it was the right choice to continue being on guard against him.

「You don’t need to be so mad at me, sniff…」

「Sei, don’t be too harsh on him. Frederie lost his lover in the Demonic Monkey Labyrinth…」

「… At any rate, I’ve truly been in your care. Let’s meet again somewhere.」

While Brai and the others are comforting the half-crying Frederie, Elmefiora and I head to where the leech is. That Frederie, it seems that in contrast to his appearance, he’s a very sensitive guy. He doesn’t seem like a bad guy, so if the opportunity arises, I guess it won’t be a bad idea to form a party with them again.

「Welcome… Ah, you are…」

I visit the leech with Elmefiora.

He is a kind-looking near-elderly man. I take out the medicinal herbs from my storage and hand them to him.

「This is amazing, they’re all of the best quality I’ve ever seen.」

「Please, I want you to compound them right away.」

「Yeah, wait a moment.」

The leech takes all the yellow silk grass and about 30% of the magic polypore and the propagating magic moss, and goes to the back of the store.

Then, we wait for about 30 minutes. I can sense a faint flow of magical energy at the back of the store, so he must be making medicine.

Fidgeting, Elmefiora seems restless and uneasy. I wonder who the medicine she is commissioning is for. I wonder if it’s for her husband, lover, or perhaps child.

「Sorry to keep you waiting.」

Coming back from the back of the store, the leech is a little out of breath, probably because he consumed a considerable amount of energy during the compounding process.

「It’s done?!」

「Yeah, here’s the anti-petrification medicine. The best quality I’ve ever made…」

「Here’s the fee!」

「Ah, Elmefiora-san.」

As soon as Elmefiora receives the medicine, she places one small gold coin on the counter and hurriedly leaves the store.

An anti-petrification medicine, huh, her adventuring comrade must have been petrified.

With this, my job is completely done. If I use the medicinal herbs I have obtained, I should be able to make high-quality stamina and magical energy restorative medicines.

「Say, will you sell me the remaining medicinal herbs?」

「Sorry, I have other plans to use these for.」

「I see, that’s a pity…」

「Besides, I believe I gave you quite a bit of magic polypore and propagating magic moss. Normally, you’re supposed to return the extra materials, no? Well, I’ll overlook it, though.」

「Th, that’s…」

I lightly intimidate the leech and then leave the store.

Compared to the palm-sized anti-petrification medicine that Elmefiora received, the amount of medicinal herbs I handed to the leech should have been on the larger side. Well, I guess it can’t be helped if he pockets a little bit of it. At least, he did his job properly, so I’ll let this one slide.

As I leave the leech’s store, I see Elmefiora running down the street.

「…」

What should I do? I’m really curious about who she’s using the medicine for.

After thinking about it for a moment, I decide to follow her.

It’s not like I want to dig out her private life or anything.

Umm, what is it, yes, I realized that I hadn’t said goodbye to her yet. I am by no means thinking of having her give form to her sense of gratitude and repay me tonight. Yes, I just want to have a little chat with her.

Using instant step, I chase after her. I almost lose sight of Elmefiora as I turn the corner, but I spot her just as she is getting into a building. I run towards the building.

「This is, an inn, huh.」

It’s a bit of a shabby inn.

It seems that Elmefiora didn’t have that much money to begin with, so she’s probably been using this inn as her regular lodging.

I step into the inn, but there seems to be no one at the reception desk. What should I do? I have no idea where she is. At that moment…

「Ares, here’s the medicine. Take it. Ares!!」

Elmefiora’s distressed voice echoes from the back of the first floor. It seems that she is in there.

As I quietly walk down the hallway, I notice that the door to the room at the very back is left open. That Elmefiora, it seems that she’s in a considerable rush.

While erasing my presence, I move to the front of the room.

「Ares, Ares, please, take this!」

「Ugh… Mother…」

When I peek into the room, I see Elmefiora struggling to make the beautiful girl lying on the bed take the anti-petrification medicine.

She’s an incredibly beautiful girl. She has almost-translucent skin, green, semi-long hair, and sparkling green eyes. And then, her most distinctive features are her ears. The beautiful girl, who is lying on the bed, and Elmefiora, who is looking after her, both have sticking out, long, pointy ears. I see, so she’s an elf. She wears a hood to hide the fact that she’s an elf.

The beautiful girl lying on the bed seems to be in a very bad condition. Her hands are petrified, and if you look closely, you can see that her neck and even part of her face are also petrified. I wonder if the medicine can really cure her from that state.

「Here, take it.」

「…gulp, gulp…」

While Elmefiora is tending to her, the beautiful girl swallows the anti-petrification medicine. Then her body starts to emit a faint light. I hope that will cure her, but…

「N, no way…」

Elmefiora’s face contorts in shock.

Due to the effect of the medicine, the petrified beauty’s face and throat have recovered from petrification, but her hands remain petrified. No matter how you slice it, it looks like the petrification has progressed too far, and medicine alone is far from enough to cure her completely.

「Uwaaaaaan, I’m sorry, Ares. Because I was too late…」

「Mother…」

「I’ll go and collect some medicinal herbs again. As long as we can get some yellow silk grasses, we should be able to make more medicines.」

Indeed, there are plenty of magic polypore and propagating magic moss. Now that I’ve seen her in such a state, I also would like to help her by all means. But I wonder if her condition will hold up until then.

「Mother, it’s enough.」

「What are you saying, Ares?」

「Please go back to Elvescoot, mother. It’s painful for me to see you suffer any more than this just because I was born with such a body. Please bury me in the demonic dragon mountain range. And then, as the legal wife of the Melfeshart family…」

「What are you saying?! You’re not to blame, Ares. I have never regretted giving birth to you, not even once. Please don’t give up on life. Ares, please…」

「Mother…」

What’s the meaning of this? It seems there’s no mistake that the beautiful girl called Ares is Elmefiora’s daughter, but… No, I’m a bit concerned about the fact that she refers to herself as 「ore」. By any chance, she’s a man? What does she mean by being born with such a body? Is the petrification something she was born with. Besides, I believe they are elves of high status, so it’s also a mystery as to why they’re staying in a place like this. There are so many things I don’t understand.

「… Who?」

「Huh, is someone there?」

Ugh, she notices me even though I’m using presence concealment. This girl, even though she’s lying on a sickbed, I wonder if she has a high proficiency level in presence detection skill.

「It’s me, Elmefiora-san.」

「Huh, Sei-kun?! Why are you here?」

「Well, I’m worried about you…」

「More importantly, please, I want you to come with me to the demonic dragon mountain range to pick some medicinal herbs again.」

Are you serious? Without Frederie and the others, it’ll be difficult for me to protect her on my own. If anything, it would probably be easier if I went to pick some yellow silk grasses on my own. But I wonder if her condition will hold up until then.

「Mother, I’m already…」

「It’s okay, just take some rest. I’ll be back soon.」

「Mother, I know my body very well. I’m going to die soon…」

「That has to be a lie! Please, Ares, I’ll be back soon. So please, please, uwaaaaaaaan.」

Elmefiora hugs her daughter while sobbing.

Although not completely, I can’t bear to watch this. With an expression as if she has sensed her death, the beautiful elven girl closes her eyes and wets her cheeks with tears. She probably doesn’t want to be a burden to her mother any longer.

Now that I’ve seen her in such a state, I guess I have no choice but to do something about it. However, as much as possible, I want to make her feel indebted to me and repay me voluntarily.

「Elmefiora-san. This…」

「Huh?! Sei-kun, don’t tell me, that’s…」

I take out a high-grade yellow potion from my storage.

Even among the potions I took from Bakumada, they are few in number, but now is probably the time to use it. If it’s this potion, it should be able to cure all abnormal status. In case it doesn’t completely cure her, I also have a gold potion with me, but since I only have one, as expected, I hesitate to use it.

「Yeah, it’s a high-grade yellow potion. It should be able to cure petrification as well.」

「Sei-kun, I beg you, I’ll do anything, so please let Ares take it…」

「Mother, please stop. There is no point in using something so precious on me. Besides, who knows how much money he would demand for it…」

The beautiful girl glares at me.

It’s painful to be looked at with disgust by a beautiful girl. From her gaze, I can sense wariness toward commonfolk. Most likely, the beautiful elven mother and daughter, who have some kind of circumstances, have gone through all sorts of bitter experiences in this town. What to do, I wonder?

「Honestly, I couldn’t care less about you.」

「What did you say…」

「I was just touched by the sight of Elmefiora-san risking her life to collect medicinal herbs for her daughter. Now, drink this before I change my mind.」

「…」

I hand the potion to Elmefiora.

「Sei-kun, thank you so, so much.」

「Yeah, give her the potion before it’s too late.」

「Yes, Ares, open your mouth.」

「Mother…」

When Elmefiora half-forcefully puts the potion in her daughter’s mouth, she obediently crushes and swallows it. Then her whole body starts to be enveloped in a light even stronger than before. This, looks like it’s going to work. Please, I absolutely do not want to use the gold potion. Please.

「This… It’s cured.」

「Ares, Ares, ah, thank God. Ares.」

「Mother, I am sorry for worrying you.」

The beautiful elven mother and daughter are crying and embracing each other. With this, they must be relieved. I used a precious potion. How on earth should I collect the payment, I wonder? From the mother… No, it was the daughter who used the potion, so from her, no, might as well from both of them. Alright, from here on is the important part. Let’s smoothly guide them into it.

「You said you were Sei, right? Thank you so much.」

「Sei-kun, thank you so much.」

「I’ll definitely thank you for this.」

「Really? You promised, alright?」

Alright, I got her words. First thing first, make sure they thank me. Then, what should I do with those thanks?

Gulp. I reflexively swallow my saliva. The sensual beauty of Elmefiora, who has taken off her hood, is a given, but her daughter’s translucent beauty is by no means inferior to hers. From the looks of it, her breasts aren’t as big as her mother’s, but I can see the curves. What should I do, which one should I aim for? As expected, both of them at the same time…

「Yeah, of course. It’s a promise between men.」

「Huh?」

# **183 - Conflict**

Between men, you say?!

What on earth is going on? Is this beautiful girl with bulging breasts by any chance a femboy? Such a ridiculous thing couldn’t be possible in this world…? No, hold on a sec. The elves of this other world are unknown existences, so it won’t be surprising that there are femboys. No, but surely…

I take another look at the beautiful elf girl called Ares, who has just recovered from an illness. She looks like a complete girl. No, there aren’t many girls as beautiful as her. Even if she is a femboy, if you were to ask me smash or nah, to be honest, I’d say smash. But, but… damn it, what should I do?

I turn my gaze to Elmefiora. As her mother, surely she could give me some kind of explanation.

# **158 - Visit to the Komatsu Family (1) ~Calling~**

According to Sayaka, the Komatsu family’s ancestry dated back to the Edo period, when they were a samurai family serving the Fudai clan in the northern part of Musashi Province.

The family was of low status and lived a rather modest life.

However, it seemed that after becoming an apprentice of a renowned swordsman and receiving the license of full mastery, they opened a dojo in the castle town and began taking students from lower-ranking retainers and townspeople.

The timeline was a little earlier than the Meiji Restoration that Yuu remembered, but the Edo Shogunate fell and a new government was established in this world as well, and the status of samurai ceased to exist.

Now that it had come to this, those who could continue to secure work as government officials were on the luckier side, but most samurai families struggled to even make ends meet.

Employing the so-called 『samurai business method』, many of them ended up increasing their debts vainly and falling into a life of poverty worse than that of the common people.

The same was true for the Komatsu family, the dojo continued to operate albeit on a small scale, but as it was no longer in the age of the sword, they began to take up employment such as soldiers and police officers, just like other samurai families.

Later on, Hanako (Sayaka’s great-grandmother), born the eldest daughter of the Komatsu family, was an eccentric girl who was a sucker for machines since childhood and became absorbed in cars and motorcycles that had just been released to the general public.

When she grew up, she became an engineer, honed her skills by working at an auto repair shop, which was rare at the time, and eventually set up her own business.

It was around this time that she met the male prostitute who would later become her husband.

Despite the ups and downs of the economy, she established a company called Komatsu Giken Kogyo (commonly known as Komatsu), and the business expanded.

「That building over there is the dojo.」

Perhaps noticing Yuu’s gaze, the woman told him as such.

Perhaps they were taking a break at the moment, or perhaps it was a day off, no voices could be heard from the inside and it was completely quiet.

「Today is Saturday, so elementary school students are expected to come at 4pm. In the evening, it’s middle and high school students. And on Sundays, adults also come.」

「Come to think of it, Sayaka said that she also trained at her home dojo until middle school. I believe the person in charge of teaching is…」

「From Sayaka-sama’s perspective, her great-aunt, Ritsuka-sama, is the instructor. She is a former police officer, and although has become a little kinder now that she has retired, back when she was still in service, she was a very strict person…」

There must have been a lot of memorable moments.

She seemed to be recalling them with a distant look in her eyes.

It seemed that the open space right in front of the dojo was also used for training. Naturally, they went barefoot even in the dead of winter.

On top of that, from spring to summer, the dojo students were also called upon to clear the weeds; she said.

Her grandmother had been an employee of Komatsu Giken since the company was founded, and even now, their families were still close with each other, and she had been training kendo in the dojo since she was a child. Even now that she was a college student majoring in physical education, she still came to the dojo on Saturdays to train.

And then, it seemed she had known Sayaka since she was a child.

「Maybe it’s because of her lineage, but she’s very competitive and hardworking. That’s why her skills in the way of the sword surpassed that of her peers. It was to such an extent that if I wasn’t careful, she might even be able to beat me, who was two years older than her. But outside the dojo, she was a very friendly and lovable person. Moreover, she had a just and upright personality, helping the weak and suppressing the strong. I would say that since she was in elementary school, you could already see a glimpse that she was someone who would stand above the masses.」

The only Sayaka that Yuu knew of was the Sayaka after she entered Sairyou Academy.

However, now that he had heard such a story, he couldn’t help but want to know what the Sayaka of the past was like.

---

「The esteemed guest has arrived.」

「Yuu-kun!」

「Hmm… Sayaka?」

Welcoming him as soon as the entrance’s sliding door was opened was Sayaka’s voice.

It seemed that she had been waiting for him, sitting in seiza on the step of the excessively spacious entrance.

Even though it was midsummer, she was dressed in a long-sleeved white blouse neatly buttoned up to the collar, with a red ribbon hanging down. On the bottom, she wore a long black skirt.

She wore her trademark long, lustrous black hair down as usual, but judging from the clean sides of her face, it looked like she had it half-up.

She was the very image of a refined young lady.

So beautiful.

He didn’t put it into words because there were other people around, but Yuu was once again captivated by her beauty.

Led by the woman who had guided them there, it was decided that the two security personnel would wait in a separate room, and Yuu, led by Sayaka, made his way to a large Japanese-style room that looked to be about 20 tatami mats in size and faced the garden.

The window facing the external corridor was thrown open, and a gentle breeze was coming in through the trees in the garden and over the pond, which was so long that it could be mistaken for a stream.

Suddenly, he heard a pleasant clacking sound.

When he looked toward the garden, he realized that it was a sound made by the shishi-odoshi (water-filled bamboo tube which clacks against a stone when emptied) that was pouring water into the pond.

Setting aside movies and dramas, this was the first time Yuu had seen one in real life, so he was overcome by a peculiar emotion.

And then, right now, sitting in seiza side by side with Sayaka, Yuu was seized by nervousness like never before.

He could tell that across the massive table carved out of a single slab of a giant tree, sitting on the left were Sayaka’s parents, and on the right were her grandparents.

「Nice to meet you. My name is Hirose Yuu. It is a pleasure to be able to meet you all, Sayaka… -san’s family, today.」

Before anyone else, Yuu offered a brief greeting and bowed to them, so all four of them showed a look of slight surprise on their faces.

「Oh my, that is very polite of you. I am Sayaka’s mother, Tomoka. Next to me is my husband, Hikaru.」

According to what Sayaka told him before, her mother, Tomoka, was the head of the marketing department at Komatsu’s head office.

She had neat short hair, perfect makeup, and was wearing a black suit on the top and bottom even though it was midsummer, which showed how flawless of a person she was.

She was the very image of a career woman who could handle her job well.

That said, she was a beautiful woman with sharp features, very much like Sayaka.

Both of her parents were probably around 40 years old.

They were the same age as Yuu prior to his rebirth, but they both had a youthful look.

While Tomoka boasted both radiant strength and beauty, it was hard to tell whether Hikaru could be called handsome, but he was a gentle and kind-looking man with a gentle, down-to-earth smile.

It didn’t seem like he was the kind of person who would angrily shout at him, 「I won’t give my daughter to you!」, even by mistake, so Yuu was relieved.

「I am Sayaka’s grandmother, Reika. This is my husband, Yoshioki.」

With her magnificent white hair tied up in a small bundle and dressed in a white kimono with a silver sash, Reika was probably at least 60 years old.

However, with her back straightened up and sharp eyes, her dignified bearing very much screamed that she was Sayaka’s grandmother.

In contrast to her small stature, she exuded an aura that she was no ordinary person from her entire body.

Perhaps this was the power of a leader who shouldered the weight of a large company.

It was a stark contrast to Sayaka’s grandfather – who was about 5 or 6 years older than her, whose hair had become completely bald from the forehead, and at a glance, gave off the impression of a good-natured old man – next to her.

In other words, while her father and grandfather were smiling and lightening the mood, her mother and grandmother, although they had a calm look on their faces, had eyes that seemed to be assessing Yuu.

They didn’t get down to business straight away, but instead amused themselves engaging in idle talks about things such as the weather that was getting hotter lately, school matters centered around Yuu and Sayaka’s work in the student council, and so on, for a while.

When Yuu praised the garden they walked through earlier, Reika began to share her extensive knowledge of gardening, and there was even a moment when she got stopped by Yoshioki as it looked like she was going to continue on forever.

A maid wearing a coverall apron brought them some cold tea, so they quenched their thirst, and as they did, the room quietened down, and the mood naturally turned into one urging them to get down to business.

「I have heard from Sayaka. It seems she’s pregnant. And the father of the child is you, Yuu-sama.」

「Yes. That’s right.」

Yuu nodded immediately at Tomoka’s words.

It’s finally here; he thought.

From here on was the real talk.

Tomoka nodded and loosened up her lips.

Seeing that no one here seemed to be rebuking her for getting pregnant, Yuu was relieved.

「With the world being as it is, it is quite the challenge for a woman to meet and get united in marriage with a man, so she has done very well. It was worth sending her to a co-ed school. I heard that although she was popular with the same sex, she was totally unpopular with the boys, after all. I heard you were younger than her, but I wonder if she had a good affinity with Yuu-sama.」

「Mother…」

As a matter of fact, it seemed that there were boys who harbored love and respect for Sayaka, but it was just that, there were none who went on the attack like Yuu; So he heard from Riko.

At any rate, so far, it looks like the flow is a welcoming one; it was understandable that Yuu thought as such.

After a short pause, he saw Tomoka take out a piece of paper.

No, on a closer look, it appeared to be not just one piece, but several pieces of paper stacked together.

Seeing that, Sayaka tilted her head. She probably hadn’t heard anything about it.

Tomoka said in a very serious tone.

「Regardless of whether it’s a boy or girl, at least, with this, the direct lineage of Komatsu won’t be severed, so it puts me at ease. The born baby will be raised as the child of the man Sayaka will eventually marry. Naturally, we will give you enough gratuity money to live a life of leisure for the of your life, so you can rest assured, Yuu-sama.」

What Tomoka presented was a contract stating that Yuu would relinquish his parental rights to the child to be born, and that he would receive a sum of gratuity money with many zeros in it, so many that he couldn’t grasp the figure right away.

+++

#  **159 - Visit to the Komatsu Family (2) ～There will be love there～**

「The born baby will be raised as the child of the man Sayaka will eventually marry. Naturally, we will give you enough gratuity money to live a life of leisure for the of your life, so you can rest assured, Yuu-sama.」

For a moment, Yuu couldn’t understand what she was saying, but gradually he got what it meant.

True enough, Sayaka had a fiancé decided by her family.

And then, Sayaka would give birth to the child in about six months.

What she was saying was that the child would be raised as the child of her fiancé, who would eventually become her husband.

As someone with the common sense from the world prior to his rebirth, he couldn’t understand it, but in this world, natural conception was considered a godsend, so it seemed that raising the child of another man while keeping the engagement, which was the bond between the families, as it was was by no means a strange thing.

Yuu ended up freezing in place, unable to say anything, but it was Sayaka who broke the silence.

「Mother! I am…」

「You should stay quiet. You know you already have a fiancé, do you not?」

「!」

「Just to make sure there is no misunderstanding, let me make it clear here, I think the fact that you have gotten pregnant is something to be celebrated. However, ultimately, you are someone who will inherit the Komatsu family, and it has been decided that you will take the son of the Osugi family as your husband.」

「Ugh… B, but, I…」

As Sayaka was at a loss for words, Tomoka turned to Yuu.

「Even if it was just a momentary whim, I am grateful that you have been willing to be Sayaka’s partner, Yuu-sama. But, you are still only 16 years old, are you not? I am sure there are plenty of girls out there for you to be with. If you could put your affairs with Sayaka behind you and continue to fulfill your duties as a man with other women from now on too…」

The contract, with a pen placed on top of it, was quietly pushed towards Yuu.

Sayaka’s father, Hikaru, didn’t not even look at him, and was turning his gaze away in a different direction.

His grandparents, Reika and Yoshioki, closed their eyes as they maintained their silence.

Which meant her mother, Tomoka, was taking the lead on this matter.

The pressure of Tomoka, who spoke while staring squarely at him, brought back Yuu’s old memories, whether he liked it or not.

The person in charge of the client who demanded an unreasonable reduction in the unit price.

The boss who, despite being aware that he was already over capacity, pushed more work onto him and went off to have a drink straight away himself.

Someone who was in a higher position and showed an arrogant attitude, anticipating the situation where the other party would not be able to refuse.

If Yuu were in a situation where he was having trouble to make a living, he might have been moved by the amount of money he saw.

However, that wasn’t what was important here.

A life born to him and Sayaka, the first person he had ever truly fallen in love with after starting his life over.

It was a dream that he had wished for so badly, and yet unable to fulfill before his rebirth.

Some might call him slow on the uptake, but there was no way he would be able to accept it.

Under everyone’s watchful eyes, Yuu, who had looked down for a while, suddenly raised his face.

And then he opened his mouth.

「N… No… I don’t want to.」

「Huh?」

「I… I… love Sayaka! Ever since I had my heart stolen by Sayaka the moment we met for the first time, the more time we spent together, the stronger my desire to be with her forever grew. The life born to me and Sayaka is mine and Sayaka’s alone. No matter how much money you offer me, there’s no way I could give up on it!」

「Yuu… -kun!」

Tears overflowed from Sayaka’s eyes as she gazed at Yuu, running down her cheeks.

Tomoka maintained her Noh mask-like expressionless face, but was it just his imagination that the gazes of Hikaru, Reika, and Yoshioki as they stared at Yuu were not threatening ones, if anything, they seemed to show a look of admiration on their faces?

「Don’t tell me, Yuu-sama, are you saying that, at such a young age, you want to take Sayaka as your wife and raise the child with her?」

「Yes, exactly as you say. I made up my mind when Sayaka told me she was pregnant. I heard that, as the other party was completely not into it, there had been no progress in her relationship with her fiancé at all. I’m confident that, compared to such a person, I will be able to make Sayaka happier!」

Before his rebirth, Yuu was unable to make even a single woman happy, but things were different now.

To date, he had exchanged feelings with a great number of women.

Among them, Sayaka, Riko, and Eimi were women he wanted to continue spending time with from now on too.

He admitted that he was being greedy, but in the first place, this was a world with a 1:30 men to women ratio.

And for Yuu, the top most existence among those 30 was Sayaka.

He had no intention of giving this up, at all.

「I see… I have certainly felt your zeal, Yuu-sama. What do you think, Sayaka?」

Having the matter directed at her, Sayaka wiped the tears that were soaking her cheeks with her fingers, smiled at Yuu when their eyes met, and then opened her mouth.

「I love Yuu-kun too. This is not a momentary feeling. As we worked together in the student council, Yuu-kun became a special existence in my heart. I couldn’t help but think about Yuu-kun all the time. It was the first time I had ever had such feelings for a boy.」

Going red in the face, Sayaka was bashful like a young girl.

Tomoka didn’t change her expression, but he could tell that Hikaru and the other two were looking at her with loving expressions.

「When I suddenly started feeling unwell in the middle of July, I was confused because I had never experienced anything like that before, but when Riko accompanied me to the obstetrics clinic and they told me that I was pregnant, a great joy welled up inside me. After understanding the reason, even the morning sickness was no longer painful. I mean, inside this belly, the life that I received from my beloved Yuu-kun is being nurtured, after all. If possible, I would like Yuu-kun to be the first to hold this child when it is born.」

Holding Sayaka’s hand as she looked at him, Yuu said.

「Likewise, I would certainly love to.」

After nodding her head, Sayaka continued.

「Besides, to me, the ideal couple is father and mother, and also grandfather and grandmother. If it is with Yuu-kun, I think we will definitely be able to become such a couple, too.」

「Oh my?!」

「Ahaha. When you put it like that, it makes me a little embarrassed.」

Reika and Yoshioki smiled at each other, while Hikaru was embarrassed.

「As the heir to the Komatsu family, I assure you. Yuu-kun is a boy who is not only excellent in appearance as you can see, but also has a rich imagination, strong mentality and a profound heart. I don’t think there is any boy who is more wonderful than him.」

Yuu was so embarrassed by the excessive praise that he blushed, but he turned to Sayaka once again and held her hands.

「Likewise, I am so happy to have met such a strong, beautiful, and wonderful woman like Sayaka. And then, I would like to continue to live side by side with her from now on too.」

「Yuu-kun…」

「Phew…」

Seeing Yuu and Sayaka looking at each other, Tomoka heaved out a breath and put her hand on her chest.

Yuu and Sayaka had no idea what that gesture signified.

She seemed to nod her head when she heard Hikaru, who was next to her, whisper something in a small voice.

Tomoka pulled the contract closer to her and at the same time raised a long, thin wooden object that she had had in her hand before they knew it.

What showed up when the sheath was quietly taken off was a shiny silver sword blade.

It was probably a pocket blade.

「M, Mother?」

Giving a sidelong glance to the shocked Yuu and Sayaka, Tomoka, still with a very serious expression on her face, held up the contract in the air and swiftly swung her pocked blade with a swish.

At a glance, it looked as if she swung it lightly from side to side, but the contract was torn into small pieces and fell to the table in a flutter.

After putting away her pocket blade, Tomoka, still in the same posture, slid back, and then straightened herself.

「Here, I have confirmed the true feelings held by Yuu-sama and Sayaka. I am terribly sorry for deliberately asking such a mean question and testing both of you.」

Tomoka bowed her head deeply.

「No. The fault lies with me here. When it was decided that we would invite Yuu-sama over, I proposed to ask him to transfer his parental rights with a fake contract, and made Tomoka play such a role, you see. I am really sorry, both of you.」

「To be honest, I certainly had some misgivings before we met, but Yuu-kun, the person Sayaka chose, is a fine young man. I’m sorry for not being able to trust my own grandchild.」

Reika, Yoshioki, and even Hikaru, who must have heard about it beforehand, all bowed their heads.

「It, it is fine… Please lift your heads!」

「Umm… I was certainly surprised, but I get it now, so!」

The four of them raised their heads at Yuu and Sayaka’s flustered words, and when their eyes met once again, they broke into a smile.

Suddenly, a question occurred to Yuu.

「Umm, what about her fiancé?」

「Ah, I suppose we have to talk about that too.」

「You’re right.」

Tomoka and Hikaru nodded to each other.

Sayaka stayed silent and assumed a listening posture.

「It’s true that strengthening our ties with the Osugi family, owners of one of the leading electronics manufacturers in Japan, would be beneficial for the Komatsu family. However, we had no thought of ignoring Sayaka’s feelings and pushing it all the way to marriage. To begin with, it was a matter that was brought up as the other party was so keen on it, so we decided to wait and see how things went until you graduated from high school. Which means, in the end, it was all up to you, Sayaka.」

「But…」

「Yes, I know. That, albeit in a clumsy manner, you have tried to get close to him. But it looks like it was only the mother who was enthusiastic, and the son, the related party, was not keen on it at all. Even if we had pushed through with the marriage, who knows if it would have worked out…」

「It depends on how Sayaka feels, but depending on the situation, we thought it might be best to break off the engagement when she graduates from high school and let her seek a new encounter, you see. Now that Sayaka has found a suitable partner, we don’t mind at all even if her engagement with the son of the Osugi family is called off. No, if anything, let us do so.」

As expected, after learning that her parents’ trains of thoughts were not so rigid that they would go as far as deciding on their daughter’s marriage just based on the benefit of the family or company, Yuu and Sayaka were relieved.

「And then, Yuu-sama.」

「Yes.」

「We didn’t have much time after hearing about you from Sayaka, but we took the liberty to look into it. The fact that your mother works for a newspaper company. And that your father is the late Toyota Sakuya-shi.」

「Huh?! D, d, don’t tell me, that…」

「Sorry, I haven’t told you about it, have I, Sayaka? That being said, it’s also only recently that I really found out about my father, though.」

When Sakuya passed away, Sayaka was only about 1 or 2 years old.

However, he was such a famous person that even now he was still regularly featured on TV and in weekly magazines, so it seemed that she knew what kind of person he was.

He had 20 official wives, and countless mistresses and women with whom he had momentary affairs. Not caring whether they were Japanese or foreign, he accepted them all.

It was certain that the children born to him numbered more than 100. Some even said it was more than 200. However, the number of boys was unknown. It was said to be 10 or 20, but the actual number was kept secret, so it was unknown.

Not only had he continued to be the object of admiration of the great majority of women since before he came of age, but he also actively moved around as the ambassador of male-female socializing.

In the end, he lost his life due to getting accidentally stabbed as he tried to settle a quarrel between his wives.

Such was the general perception of him.

「Yuu-kun’s father was… that Toyota Sakuya-shi…」

With the person in question right in front of her, Sayaka recalled Yuu’s actions thus far, and she was readily convinced that his bloodline had definitely been passed down.

「Marriage is not just about the feelings of the two people involved, it’s also about relationships between the families, you see. In that respect, even now, there are still voices of admiration for Sakuya among the middle and young ranks of the political and business world, after all.」

「Yes, in that sense, creating ties with Yuu-sama is something the Komatsu family would greatly welcome, so we would never consider rejecting it.」

Reika and Tomoka both looked at Yuu.

Their expressions were completely different from before, and it was clear that they were expressing their welcome.

As for Yuu, he was inwardly surprised that his father’s name had popped up even here.

He had heard many things about his father whom he had never met, but honestly speaking, he didn’t know how he should feel about him.

However, to women of a certain generation, he was undoubtedly treated as an idol or a legend.

As it had a positive effect on him, perhaps he could only welcome it.

「Err… In any case, could I take it that you allow my relationships with Sayaka?」

「Yes, of course. Please take good care of Sayaka.」

「Yes! I’ll make her happy!」

「Yuu-kun!」

Yuu’s love for Sayaka only grew as she clung to his arm tightly.

He wanted to continue embracing her just like that, but as expected, he was hesitant to do so in front of her family.

「That reminds me. I believe it was towards the end of Tomoka’s second year in college.」

「Huh?!」

「You’re right. She suddenly brought Hikaru-kun over and said, 『I’m going to marry this guy!』. Until then, she hadn’t showed any interest in men at all, so it truly was like a bolt out of the blue.」

「Yup, yup. Six months later, her belly started to swell.」

「T-t-t, there’s no need to talk about me!」

「But I was the one who confessed to her, you know. At first, I thought she was cool, not just beautiful, but also quick-witted and confident, but when we were alone, she had a really cute side.」

「D, dear!」

It seemed that even Tomoka was embarrassed when her past prior to their marriage was brought up.

Her face turned bright red and she started hitting Hikaru to stop him from talking.

The scene looked like nothing but flirting.

「Then, grandfather, grandmother, how did your two meet and end up getting married?」

「Us, huh. You see, we were actually childhood friends who lived in the same neighborhood.」

「Childhood friends?!」

「And then, and then?」

「Since we’re at this already, tell us how you two got together, too!」

As Sayaka suddenly turned the spotlight to them, Reika was startled and thought about silencing her husband, but it seemed she was too late.

Yoshioki began to talk with a wide smile on his face, and not only Yuu and Sayaka, but even Tomoka, who welcomed the change of topic, listened with great interest.

「You see, since I was in elementary school, I went to Komatsu’s dojo to learn kendo even though I was a boy. Unfortunately, my skills didn’t improve much, so I decided to quit when I graduated from elementary school. Then, a girl who was skilled enough to compete for the first place among the lower grades of elementary school at the time said this to me. 『Onii-sama, I will protect you. So please be at ease.』」

「「「Ooh!」」」

「S, stop it…」

This time, Reika’s face turned bright red and she ended up casting her eyes down.

「Back then, with the exception of a few wealthy families, it wasn’t customary for middle school boys to have guards accompanying them to and from school. At most, they would have their mothers, who had time to spare, take them to and from school. In those days, there weren’t many houses around this area, and it was pitch black at night, making it dangerous, so Reika took the trouble of taking a detour to accompany me to and from school. The following year, her younger sister Ritsuka also joined us. The sisters did actually fend off suspicious adults that showed up near my house, you know? There’s no way I wouldn’t find such reliable and cute childhood friends lovely. As we continued to spend time together for years, we fell in love with each other for real, and when Reika turned 18 and Ritsuka turned 17, I proposed to them.」

「Ufufu. Grandmother and grandaunt are…」

「Wh, what is it?」

「You’re so lovely!」

「You’re right. I think so, too.」

As the atmosphere took one eighty and turned into one full of smiles, Yuu recalled the words he had heard the other day.

「According to the traditions of the Komatsu family, Yuu-kun is more suitable.」

So Riko had said.

In other words, for generations, the couples of the Komatsu family had been united in marriage after falling in love with each other while they were still young and eventually had children.

Yuu wrapped his arm around Sayaka’s shoulder and murmured.

「How nice. I want to become a family with such wonderful people; that’s my honest thought now.」

「Yuu-kun…Thank you.」

Overcome with emotion, Sayaka closed her eyes, and rested her head on Yuu’s shoulder.

+++

# **160 - Visit to the Komatsu Family (3) ~The Room, the Y-Shirt, and Me~**

The chatting continued in a relaxed atmosphere for a while, but eventually, they decided to set a date for the guardians of not only Yuu and Sayaka, but also Riko and Eimi to meet in order to seal their engagement.

The planned date was Sunday, August 12th.

Yuu could have asked Martina, but Sayaka’s mother, Tomoka, took upon herself the role of organizing the meeting, and said she wanted to greet and have a talk with them first, so he decided to leave it to her.

Incidentally, it seemed that Tomoka knew about Riko and Emi as well.

Having three fiancées at the age of 16, he was praised, 「as expected of Sakuya-shi’s son」, which he found peculiar.

In this world, it wasn’t like there were no boys who were in a relationship with the intention of getting married while they were still minors (under 18), but it was extremely rare for a boy to already be in a relationship with three girls and even have children with them at such age.

It was to such an extent even for these people, the only ones they knew were Sakuya and Yuu.

If the tale of Yuu, who had sowed his seeds not only in those three, but in a large number of women, became more well known, it would not be surprising even if people called him the second coming of Sakuya.

It was almost 4pm when the conversation came to a close.

Given the occasion, they invited him to dinner.

Yuu thought about declining, but as Sayaka also joined them in inviting him, it became difficult to refuse, so in the end he decided to accept.

However, it seemed that Reika alone had to go out for work.

Having a meal with your girlfriend’s family whom you had just met, under normal circumstances, not being nervous about it would be the strange one, but perhaps because he had talked with them for about two hours, he felt that they had opened up to each other quite a bit.

The main reason they had opened up to such an extent, even though Yuu himself was not someone who was good at communicating by nature, was that Sayaka’s father and grandfather were extremely friendly people.

When Yuu, as requested, called them 「mother-in-law」 and 「father-in-law」, Hikaru and Tomoka were delighted, feeling as if they had a son.

As such, he also started calling Reika and Yoshioki 「Grandma-in-law」 and 「Grandpa-in-law」.

In return, Yuu asked them to stop speaking in a distant manner, such as attaching -sama to his name and speaking in a formal manner.

---

While waiting for dinner to be prepared, as it was a good chance, Yuu asked to spend the time in the room Sayaka used to use.

Even though he had formed deep relationships with a great number of women thus far, Sayaka was the only one whose room he had ever visited.

It was a world where boys could not go out to play casually, so that was inevitable, though.

As such, he wanted to take a look at her room in her parents’ house as well.

The second floor appeared to have been added later, and the interior was brighter than the first floor, and the hallway, walls, and window frames also seemed new.

When he saw it from outside, the second floor seemed small compared to the first floor, but now that he had actually gone there, it seemed to be much larger than an average house.

Not only were there three doors along the hallway right after going up the stairs, it seemed to still be stretching on beyond the corner.

「This is the room I used until middle school.」

「T, then… pardon the intrusion.」

His first impression of the 8-tatami room was that it was so neat and tidy.

It seemed to have been thoroughly cleaned, and there wasn’t even a single hair or speck of dust on the tatami.

There were few possessions and no decorations, so he couldn’t feel any hint of life.

That, too, was probably inevitable.

Since it had been two and a half years since she moved her base of living to an apartment in Saiou City.

Partly because there was no bed, and the bedding was stored in the closet, it was extra spacious.

The only things that stood out were the massive Japanese dresser that appeared to be something from the old era, and the study desk that she used until middle school.

The navy blazer and skirt hanging on a hanger by the wall were probably her middle school uniform.

Framed certificates of merit were hanging on the lintel, allowing him to get a glimpse of her glory as captain of the kendo club, such as winning the prefectural tournament.

「How is it? I don’t think it’s very interesting, though.」

「No, that’s not true at all.」

Sure, it was far from the image of a girl’s room that Yuu imagined.

The vice presidents could concurrently hold a position in clubs or various committees, but for generations, the president alone was a full-time member and couldn’t engage in any extracellular activities.

「Oioi. You’re putting him in trouble there. Just let him go already.」

Suddenly, they heard a man’s voice from the direction of the door.

Satsuki, who went 「Hmm」 and turned around, reluctantly let go of Yuu.

Over her shoulder, she saw a man, probably around 30 years old, standing there.

「Ma-kun you meanie. Isn’t it fine? He’s the little brother I’ve met for the first time, you know? Moreover, even though it was our first meeting, he called me a pretty big sister. There’s no way it won’t me happy, is there?!」

「Well, I get that, but… I heard he’s still only 16 years old, you know? You’re being too clingy with your little brother, who is half your age, from the get-go.」

「It’s fine! I just turned 30, so I’m not twice as old, duh!」

「Huh, big sis Satsuki, you’re 30? I thought you were 25 or so.」

Women in their late 20s and beyond, which is said to be the turning point for their skin, are all happy to be seen as young.

As such, when asked how old you think she is, it’s best to lower the age you honestly think by a few years; Yuu remembered being told so in the past.

However, if you were too far off the mark, it would come across as a lie, so the difficult part was to find the right balance.

As soon as Satsuki heard Yuu’s words, her eyes widened, and she put her hand over her mouth, revealing her surprise. At the same time, the corners of her eyes, which were droopy, drooped even further.

「See! Did you hear that?! Oh you, Yuu, not only are you good-looking, you also have a kind personality, so lovely!」

As expected, this time she didn’t hug him from the front, but instead took his right arm and held it tightly with both hands.

Even though she was his half-blood elder sister, there was no way he wouldn’t be happy to have a male-instincts-stirring sexy beautiful woman press her breasts against him.

However, there, Yuu decided to hide his inner joy and face the man who had come after Satsuki.

「Ah, sorry for the late introduction. My name is Masaki. I’m 29 years old, so I’m much older than you, but I’m your older brother.」

「Err, my name is… Yuu. Nice to meet you.」

「No polite speech, okay?」

「Ah, I see. Best regards, big brother.」

「Likewise, best regards, little brother.」

The nameplate hanging around his neck read, 『Member No. STC.006 Masaki』.

Masaki and Yuu exchanged greetings and shook hands firmly.

He was about the same height as Yuu and had a slender figure.

He was wearing a black and white striped long-sleeved shirt buttoned up to his neck, and dark grey slacks.

His skin was fair, and his slightly long hair was closer to brown than black.

He was a handsome man who strongly inherited the looks of their father, whom he had only seen in photos, and his characteristic was his gentle eyes.

They were 13 years apart in age, but being face to face with him like this, he keenly felt that he was someone related to him by blood, and for some reason it made him feel nostalgic.

「It’s kind of strange. I’d heard that I had brothers, but to think that we’d actually meet like this…」

「You’re right. And it’s exactly because brothers are rare in this world that I’d like to cherish this kind of bond.」

「I’m terribly sorry to interrupt you during your emotional meeting, but shall we come inside soon?」

「「Ah.」」

Getting urged by Hiromi, they realized something…

The fact that they had completely forgotten about these girls.

Through the door Masaki and Satsuki had opened for them, Yuu’s group finally stepped into the facility.
